        switch (level) {
            case 0:
                dic0 = _.find(dictionaries, { ID: id })         //Hàm _.find () xem xét từng phần tử của danh sách và trả về lần xuất hiện đầu tiên của phần tử thỏa mãn điều kiện

                }

                renderDicImageItems(dic2, '.btn__category--child__new__lv2 .dic__image')

                renderDicItems(dic2, '.btn__category--child__new__lv3 .dic__content', '.btn__category--child__new__lv3 .dic__title', 3)
                renderDicImageItems(dic2, '.btn__category--child__new__lv3 .dic__image')
                break
            case 3:
                dic3 = _.find(dic2.Items, { ID: id })

                renderDicImageItems(dic3, '.btn__category--child__new__lv3 .dic__image')
                break
        }
    }

    const renderDicItems = (data, className, classTitle, level) => {
        $(className).empty()
        let title = ''
        if (data) {
            
            data.Items.map(o => {
                $(className).append(`<a type="button" class="btn w-100 p-2 pe-1 text-start btn-dictionary--tab__new" data-level="${level}" data-id="${o.ID}" href="${o.Link}">
                                            <span class="btn__category--title__new pe-2">${o.Ten}</span>
                                        </a>`)
            })

            title = data.Ten
            if (data.Items.length) {
                $(className).parent().removeClass("d-none")
            } else {
                if (!$(className).parent().hasClass("d-none")) {
                    $(className).parent().addClass("d-none")
                }
            }
        }
        $(classTitle).text(title)
    }
    const renderDicImageItems = (data, className) => {
        $(className).empty()
        if (data && data.PictureBAA) {
            let path
            if (data.isDirectory == "1" && (data.ID == data.ParentID || data.ParentID == "0")) {
                path = vbPathDirectory300
            } else if (data.isDirectory == "1" && data.ID != data.ParentID) {
                path = vbPathDirectory300
            } else {
                path = vbPathCategory300
            }
            $(className).append(`<img class="dic-img-picture" src="${path}${data.PictureBAA}" />`)
        }
    }

    const renderLinkDic = (id, isDirectory, parentID, idCategory) => {
        let data = {}
        if (isDirectory == "1" && (id == parentID || parentID == "0")) {
            data = renderProductsDicData(id)
        } else if (isDirectory == "1" && id != parentID) {
            data = renderProductsDicData(null, id)
        } else {
            data = renderProductsDicData(null, id, idCategory)
        }
        return vbLink + productsConvertUrl(data, true)
    }

    const activeDic = () => {
        if (vbDic || vbCate || vbGroup) {
            const childDic = vbCate ? $(`.tree-block[data-idcategory="${vbCate}"]`) : vbGroup ? $(`.tree-block[data-id="${vbGroup}"]`) : $(`.tree-block[data-id="${vbDic}"]`)
            if (childDic.length) {
                childDic.find(">:first-child a").addClass("fw-bold")
                childDic.parents('.tree-block').addClass('show')
            }
        }
    }

    


    $(document).ready(function () {
        
        $(`.btns__categories__new`).on('mouseenter', '.btn-dictionary--tab__new', function () {                  // mouseenter: sự kiện khi di chuột vào class "btns__categories__new"
            const level = $(this).data('level')
            renderDic(level, $(this).data('id'))
        }).on('mouseleave', '.btn-dictionary--tab__new', function () {                                           // mouseleave: sự kiện khi di chuột ra class "btns__categories__new" sẽ tác động lên class "dic__content"
            $('btn__category--child__new .dic__content').empty()
        })

        // Fix size
        const screenSize = window.innerWidth
        //console.log(screenSize)
        if (screenSize <= 600) {

        } else if (screenSize < 1086) {
            $('.btn__category--child__new').css("width", "230px")
            $('.btn__category--child__new__lv2').css("left", "528px")
            $('.btn__category--child__new__lv3').css("left", "758px")
        } else if (screenSize < 1300) {
            $('.btn__category--child__new').css("width", "250px")
            $('.btn__category--child__new__lv2').css("left", "548px")
            $('.btn__category--child__new__lv3').css("left", "798px")
        } else if (screenSize < 1420) {
            $('.btn__category--child__new').css("width", "300px")
            $('.btn__category--child__new__lv2').css("left", "598px")
            $('.btn__category--child__new__lv3').css("left", "898px")
        } else if (screenSize < 1710) {
            $('.btn__category--child__new').css("width", "350px")
            $('.btn__category--child__new__lv2').css("left", "648px")
            $('.btn__category--child__new__lv3').css("left", "998px")
        }



        // Mobile

        $('.dictionary__mobile .tree-more').on('click', function () {
            if ($(this).parent().parent().hasClass("show")) {
                $(this).parent().parent().removeClass('show')
            } else {
                $(this).parent().parent().addClass('show')
            }
        })

        // active folder
        activeDic()
    })

</script>

                    if (lst.length) {
                        for (i = 0; i < lst.length  ; i++) {
                            if ($.inArray(`${lst[i]}`, loadLst) == -1) {  // Lấy các Spec vào loadLst và loại bỏ Spec trùng lặp
                                loadLst.push(`${lst[i]}`)
                                if (loadLst.length == 50) {
                                    break
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                if (loadLst.length) {
                    initFilterTop += loadLst.length
                    for (i = 0; i < loadLst.length; i++) {
                        apiFilterboxOne(vbSeri, cate, loadLst[i], data.ls, inputs, i + 3)
                    }

                    initFilterTopHtml[1] = vbhtmlFilterCate

                    apiFilterCategory(vbSeri, cate, data.ls, inputs, 1)

                if (vbhtmlFilterSeries != '') {
                    initFilterTopHtml[2] = vbhtmlFilterSeries
                } else {
                    apiFilterSeries(vbSeri, cate, data.ls, inputs, 2)
                }
                initFilterTopHtml[initFilterTop] = filterTopAddBtn
                apiFilterboxManufacturer(vbSeri, cate, data.ls, inputs, 0)
            }
        }
        const getAddFilter = () => {
            var isCateSeri = ''

                            } else {
                                apiFilterSeries(vbSeri, cate, data.ls, inputs, 2)
                            }
                        } else {
                            apiFilterboxOne(vbSeri, cate, loadLst[i], data.ls, inputs, i  )
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        const renderModels = (data) => {
            $(".models-loading").empty()
            data.map(o => {
                let price = ``
                let ship = ``
                if (o.GiaBanMinMOQInt != null && o.GiaBanMinMOQInt != 0 && (o.SLMOQ1 != null || o.SLMOQ2 != null || o.SLMOQ3 != null)) {
                    price += `<div class="product__card--price">`
                    if (o.SLKhuyenMai != null && o.SLKhuyenMai > 0 && o.SLKhuyenMai > o.SLMOQ1) {       // Hiển thị giá Khuyến mại tùy theo số lượng MOQ, SLKM phải > SLMOQ thấp nhất
                        if (o.SLKhuyenMai > o.SLMOQ3) {
                            price += `<span class="fw-bold text-danger text-start">${o.GiaBanMOQ3}${vbVNUnit} `
                        } else if (o.SLKhuyenMai > o.SLMOQ2) {
                            price += `<span class="fw-bold text-danger text-start">${o.GiaBanMOQ2}${vbVNUnit} `
                        } else {
                            price += `<span class="fw-bold text-danger text-start">${o.GiaBanMOQ1}${vbVNUnit} `
                        }
                    } else if (o.SLKhuyenMai != null && o.SLKhuyenMai > 0 && o.SLKhuyenMai < o.SLMOQ1) {        // SLKM nhỏ hơn MOQ nhỏ nhất => Giá cho 1 cái
                        price += `<span class="fw-bold text-danger text-start">${utilsFormatNum3(o.DonGiaMax)}${vbVNUnit} `
                    }
                    else if (o.SLMOQ1) {     // Phải có MOQ thấp nhất
                        if (o.SLMOQ3) {
                            price += `<span class="fw-bold text-danger text-start">${o.GiaBanMOQ3}${vbVNUnit} `
                        } else if (o.SLMOQ2) {
                            price += `<span class="fw-bold text-danger text-start">${o.GiaBanMOQ2}${vbVNUnit} `
                        } else if (o.SLMOQ1) {
                            price += `<span class="fw-bold text-danger text-start">${o.GiaBanMOQ1}${vbVNUnit} `
                        }
                    } else {
                        price += `<span class="fw-bold text-danger text-start">${utilsFormatNum3(o.DonGiaMax)}${vbVNUnit} `     // (1)
                    }
                    if (vbIdentityUserID && ((o.SLKhuyenMai == null && o.SLMOQ1 && o.SLMOQ1 > 0) || (o.SLKhuyenMai && o.SLKhuyenMai > 0 && o.SLKhuyenMai >= o.SLMOQ1))) {
                        if (o.ApdungGiaUser) {
                            if (o.GiaUserDacBietInt && o.GiaUserDacBietInt != 0) {
                                price += `~ ${o.GiaUserDacBiet}${vbVNUnit}`
                            } else if (o.GiaBanUserInt) {
                                price += `~ ${o.GiaBanUser}${vbVNUnit}`
                            }
                        } else if (o.SLKhuyenMai > 0) {
                            price += `~ ${o.GiaBanKhuyenMai}${vbVNUnit}`
                        } else if (o.BuocGiaTot != 0) {
                            price += `~ ${o.GiaBanTot}${vbVNUnit}`

        const checkToShowModelFilter = (checkStock, checkNew, checkSale, checkGood, filterParams, TangGiam, LoadModel) => {
            let inputs = []
            var currentUrl = window.location.search
            let ThamSoSplit = currentUrl.replace('?', '')
            let arrThamSoSplit = ThamSoSplit.split("&")
            for (i = 0; i < arrThamSoSplit.length; i++) {
                if (arrThamSoSplit[i].includes(`params=`)) {
                    let cancelText = arrThamSoSplit[i].split("_")[0]
                    var params = cancelText.replace('params=', '').split(';')
                    params.forEach(function (param) {
                        var paramArr = param.split(':')
                        var paramName = paramArr[0]
                        var paramValue = paramArr[1]
                        for (i = 0; i < 120; i++) {
                            if (paramName == (i)) {
                                inputs.push({
                                    Col: i,
                                    IDs: paramValue.split(',')
                                })
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
            var LocCoSan = ``
            var spNewSaleGood = ``
            var SapXepThongSo = ``
            var SapXepTheoOrderBy = ``
            if (checkStock) {     
                LocCoSan += ` sp.TonBAC > 0 `
            }
            if (checkNew) {
                    spNewSaleGood = `moi`
            } else if (checkSale) {
                    spNewSaleGood = `khuyen-mai`
            } else if (checkGood) {
                spNewSaleGood = `gia-tot`
            }
            if (TangGiam == '1') {     
                SapXepTheoOrderBy += 'DESC'
            }
            var vbHangSX = []
            if (vbIDHangSX) {
                vbHangSX.push(vbIDHangSX)
            }
            axios.post(`/api/UtilsApi/sap-xep-models-order-price`, { lang: vbLang, IDs: models, filter: { List: spNewSaleGood, Cate: vbCate, Group: vbGroup, Dic: vbDic, Seri: vbSeri, Spec: inputs, HangSX: vbHangSX }, CoSan: ` sp.TonBAC > 0 `, SapXepThongSo: SapXepThongSo, orderby: SapXepTheoOrderBy })
                    .then(function (response) {
                        if (response.data.data) {
                            $('.countModelsCoSan').empty()
                            $('.countModelsCoSan').append('[' + response.data.Count + ']')
                            $('.countModelsCoSan').attr('data-count', response.data.Count)
                            if (response.data.Count > 0 && !vbActiveView) {
                                $('#checkerLableAvailable').attr('disabled', false)
                            } else {
                                $('#checkerLableAvailable').attr('disabled', true)
                            }
                        } else {
                            $('#checkerLableAvailable').attr('disabled', true)
                            $('.countModelsCoSan').empty()
                            $('.countModelsCoSan').append('[0]');
                        }
                    })
                axios.post(`/api/UtilsApi/sap-xep-models-order-price`, { lang: vbLang, IDs: models, filter: { List: `moi`, Cate: vbCate, Group: vbGroup, Dic: vbDic, Seri: vbSeri, Spec: inputs, HangSX: vbHangSX }, CoSan: LocCoSan, SapXepThongSo: SapXepThongSo, orderby: SapXepTheoOrderBy })
                .then(function (response) {
                    if (response.data.data) {
                        $('.countModelsMoi').empty()
                        $('.countModelsMoi').append('[' + response.data.Count + ']')
                        $('.countModelsMoi').attr('data-count', response.data.Count)
                        if (response.data.Count == 0) {
                            $('#checkerLableNew').attr('disabled', true)
                        }
                    } else {
                        $('#checkerLableNew').attr('disabled', true)
                        $('.countModelsMoi').empty()
                        $('.countModelsMoi').append('[0]')
                    }
                })
                axios.post(`/api/UtilsApi/sap-xep-models-order-price`, { lang: vbLang, IDs: models, filter: { List: `khuyen-mai`, Cate: vbCate, Group: vbGroup, Dic: vbDic, Seri: vbSeri, Spec: inputs, HangSX: vbHangSX }, CoSan: LocCoSan, SapXepThongSo: SapXepThongSo, orderby: SapXepTheoOrderBy })
                .then(function (response) {
                    if (response.data.data) {
                        $('.countModelsKhuyenMai').empty()
                        $('.countModelsKhuyenMai').append('[' + response.data.Count + ']')
                        $('.countModelsKhuyenMai').attr('data-count', response.data.Count)
                        if (response.data.Count == 0) {
                            $('#checkerLableSale').attr('disabled', true)
                        }
                    } else {
                        $('#checkerLableSale').attr('disabled', true)
                        $('.countModelsKhuyenMai').empty()
                        $('.countModelsKhuyenMai').append('[0]');
                    }
                })
                axios.post(`/api/UtilsApi/sap-xep-models-order-price`, { lang: vbLang, IDs: models, filter: { List: `gia-tot`, Cate: vbCate, Group: vbGroup, Dic: vbDic, Seri: vbSeri, Spec: inputs, HangSX: vbHangSX }, CoSan: LocCoSan, SapXepThongSo: SapXepThongSo, orderby: SapXepTheoOrderBy })
                .then(function (response) {
                    if (response.data.data) {
                        $('.countModelsGiaTot').empty()
                        $('.countModelsGiaTot').append('[' + response.data.Count + ']')
                        $('.countModelsGiaTot').attr('data-count', response.data.Count)
                        if (response.data.Count == 0) {
                            $('#checkerLableGood').attr('disabled', true)
                        }
                    } else {
                        $('#checkerLableGood').attr('disabled', true)
                        $('.countModelsGiaTot').empty()
                        $('.countModelsGiaTot').append('[0]');
                    }
                })
            if (LoadModel == `1`) {
                HideModelPhanTrangOld()

                if (filterParams == 100001) {              
                    SapXepThongSo = ` sp.TonBac `
                } else if (filterParams == 100002) {        
                    SapXepThongSo = ` thsx.TEN `
                } else if (filterParams == 100003) {       
                    SapXepThongSo = `GiaToiThieu`
                } else if (filterParams == 100004) {      
                    SapXepThongSo = `GiaToiDa`
                } else if (filterParams == 100005) {      
                    SapXepThongSo = ` sp.Model `
                }
                axios.post(`/api/UtilsApi/sap-xep-models-order-price`, { lang: vbLang, IDs: models, filter: { List: spNewSaleGood, Cate: vbCate, Group: vbGroup, Dic: vbDic, Seri: vbSeri, Spec: inputs, HangSX: vbHangSX }, CoSan: LocCoSan, SapXepThongSo: SapXepThongSo, orderby: SapXepTheoOrderBy })
                    .then(function (response) {
                        if (response.data.data) {
                            $('.countModels').empty()
                            $('.countModels').append(response.data.Count);
                            var idModels = response.data.data.split(",")
                            const tongSotrang = Math.ceil(idModels.length / 20)
                            $('#products-tab').attr('data-ids', "")
                            $('#products-tab').attr('data-ids', response.data.data)
                            modelLoadPageOrderby(modelsPageOrder, idModels)
                            $('#page-selection-orderby').twbsPagination({
                                totalPages: tongSotrang,
                                startPage: 1,
                                visiblePages: 5,
                                first: 'First',
                                prev: '<',
                                next: '>',
                                last: 'Last',
                                href: false,
                                pageClass: "page-item",
                                anchorClass: "page-link",
                                onPageClick: (e, page) => {
                                    let idsModel = $('#products-tab').attr('data-ids').split(",")
                                    modelLoadPageOrderby(page, idsModel)
                                    //$('html, body').animate({
                                    //    scrollTop: $("#products-tab").offset().top
                                    //}, 200)
                                }
                            });
                            if (startFilterNew == 1) {
                                $('#page-selection-orderby').twbsPagination('destroy')
                                $('#page-selection-orderby').twbsPagination({
                                    totalPages: tongSotrang,
                                    startPage: 1,
                                    visiblePages: 5,
                                    first: 'First',
                                    prev: '<',
                                    next: '>',
                                    last: 'Last',
                                    href: false,
                                    pageClass: "page-item",
                                    anchorClass: "page-link",
                                    onPageClick: (e, page) => {
                                        let idsModel = $('#products-tab').attr('data-ids').split(",")
                                        modelLoadPageOrderby(page, idsModel)
                                        //$('html, body').animate({
                                        //    scrollTop: $("#products-tab").offset().top
                                        //}, 200)
                                    }
                                })
                                return
                            }
                        }
                    })
            }

        const customDatatables = () => {
            $('#orderbyParams').on('processing.dt', function (e, settings, processing) {
                if (!$(".loadingGridGray").hasClass('d-none')) {
                    $('.loadingGridGray').addClass('d-none')
                }
                if ($("#orderbyParams").hasClass('d-none')) {
                    $('#orderbyParams').removeClass('d-none')
                }
            }).DataTable({
                fixedColumns: {
                    left: 2
                },
                initComplete: function () {             // off autocompsearch
                    $(this.api().table().container()).find('input').parent().wrap('<form>').parent().attr('autocomplete', 'off');
                },
                columnDefs:
                    [
                        { type: "num-custom", targets: "_all" }
                    ],
                oLanguage: {
                    oAria: {
                        sSortAscending: ": activate to sort column ascending", sSortDescending: ": activate to sort column descending"
                    },
                    oPaginate: {
                        sFirst: "First", sLast: "Last", sNext: `${vbLang == `vn` ? `Sau` : `Next`}`, sPrevious: `${vbLang == `vn` ? `Trước` : `Prev`}`
                    },
                    sEmptyTable: "No data available in table",
                    sInfo: `${vbLang == `vn` ? `Đang xem _START_ đến _END_ trong tổng số _TOTAL_ mục` : `Viewing _START_ to _END_ of _TOTAL_ items`}`,
                    sInfoEmpty: "Showing 0 to 0 of 0 entries",
                    sInfoFiltered: "(filtered from _MAX_ total entries)",
                    sInfoPostFix: "",
                    sDecimal: "",
                    sThousands: ",",
                    sLengthMenu: `${vbLang == `vn` ? `Xem _MENU_ mục` : `View _MENU_ items`}`,
                    sLoadingRecords: "Loading...",
                    sProcessing: "",
                    sSearch: `${vbLang == `vn` ? `Tìm kiếm:` : `Search:`}`,
                    sSearchPlaceholder: "",
                    sUrl: "",
                    sZeroRecords: "No matching records found"
                }
            });
            // Thêm một loại dữ liệu số thực tùy chỉnh vào DataTables
            jQuery.extend(jQuery.fn.dataTableExt.oSort, {
                "num-custom-pre": function (a) {
                    var element = $(a)
                    var content = element.filter('.text_td').text();
                    // Kiểm tra xem chuỗi có số đứng đầu không
                    if (/^\d/.test(content)) {
                        // Nếu có, loại bỏ tất cả các ký tự không phải số hoặc dấu chấm và chuyển đổi thành số thực
                        var number = parseFloat(content.replace(/[^\d.]/g, ''));
                        return isNaN(number) ? 0 : number;
                    } else {
                        // Nếu không, giữ nguyên chuỗi
                        return content == `-` ? `` : content
                    }
                },
                "nume-custom-asc": function (a, b) {
                    var $a = $(a)
                    var $b = $(b)
                    var content_a = $a.filter('.text_td').text();
                    var content_b = $b.filter('.text_td').text();
                    // Kiểm tra xem a và b có số đứng đầu không
                    var isANumeric = /^\d/.test(content_a);
                    var isBNumeric = /^\d/.test(content_b);

                    if (isANumeric && isBNumeric) {
                        // Nếu cả hai đều có số đứng đầu, so sánh như số thực
                        return parseFloat(content_a) - parseFloat(content_b);
                    } else if (isANumeric) {
                        // Nếu chỉ a có số đứng đầu, a đứng sau b
                        return 1;
                    } else if (isBNumeric) {
                        // Nếu chỉ b có số đứng đầu, a đứng trước b
                        return -1;
                    } else {
                        // Nếu cả hai đều không có số đứng đầu, so sánh bình thường
                        return (content_a > content_b) ? 1 : ((content_a < content_b) ? -1 : 0);
                    }
                },
                "nume-custom-desc": function (a, b) {
                    var $a = $(a)
                    var $b = $(b)
                    var content_a = $a.filter('.text_td').text();
                    var content_b = $b.filter('.text_td').text();
                    // Sử dụng hàm sắp xếp tăng dần với thứ tự đảo ngược
                    return jQuery.fn.dataTableExt.oSort["numeric-custom-asc"](content_b, content_a);
                }
            });
        }
        const showModelGridToBlock = (checkStock, checkNew, checkSale, checkGood, filterParams, TangGiam) => {
            let inputs = []
            var currentUrl = window.location.search
            let ThamSoSplit = currentUrl.replace('?', '')
            let arrThamSoSplit = ThamSoSplit.split("&")
            for (i = 0; i < arrThamSoSplit.length; i++) {
                if (arrThamSoSplit[i].includes(`params=`)) {
                    let cancelText = arrThamSoSplit[i].split("_")[0]
                    var params = cancelText.replace('params=', '').split(';')
                    params.forEach(function (param) {
                        var paramArr = param.split(':')
                        var paramName = paramArr[0]
                        var paramValue = paramArr[1]
                        for (i = 0; i < 120; i++) {
                            if (paramName == (i)) {
                                inputs.push({
                                    Col: i,
                                    IDs: paramValue.split(',')
                                })
                            }
                        }
                    });
                }
            }
            var LocCoSan = ``
            var spNewSaleGood = ``
            var SapXepThongSo = ``
            var SapXepTheoOrderBy = ``
            if (checkStock) {
                LocCoSan += ` sp.TonBAC > 0 `
            }
            if (checkNew) {
                spNewSaleGood = `moi`
            } else if (checkSale) {
                spNewSaleGood = `khuyen-mai`
            } else if (checkGood) {
                spNewSaleGood = `gia-tot`
            }
            if (TangGiam == '1') {
                SapXepTheoOrderBy += 'DESC'
            }
            var vbHangSX = []
            if (vbIDHangSX) {
                vbHangSX.push(vbIDHangSX)
            }
            if (ReloadBlockModels == 1) {
                HideModelPhanTrangOld()
                if (filterParams == 100001) {
                    SapXepThongSo = ` sp.TonBac `
                } else if (filterParams == 100002) {
                    SapXepThongSo = ` thsx.TEN `
                } else if (filterParams == 100003) {
                    SapXepThongSo = `GiaToiThieu`
                } else if (filterParams == 100004) {
                    SapXepThongSo = `GiaToiDa`
                } else if (filterParams == 100005) {
                    SapXepThongSo = ` sp.Model `
                }
                axios.post(`/api/UtilsApi/sap-xep-models-order-price`, { lang: vbLang, IDs: models, filter: { List: spNewSaleGood, Cate: vbCate, Group: vbGroup, Dic: vbDic, Seri: vbSeri, Spec: inputs, HangSX: vbHangSX }, CoSan: LocCoSan, SapXepThongSo: SapXepThongSo, orderby: SapXepTheoOrderBy })
                    .then(function (response) {
                        if (response.data.data) {
                            $('.countModels').empty()
                            $('.countModels').append(response.data.Count);
                            var idModels = response.data.data.split(",")
                            const tongSotrang = Math.ceil(idModels.length / 20)
                            $('#products-tab').attr('data-ids', "")
                            $('#products-tab').attr('data-ids', response.data.data)
                            modelLoadPageOrderby(modelsPageOrder, idModels)
                            $('#page-selection-orderby').twbsPagination({
                                totalPages: tongSotrang,
                                startPage: 1,
                                visiblePages: 5,
                                first: 'First',
                                prev: '<',
                                next: '>',
                                last: 'Last',
                                href: false,
                                pageClass: "page-item",
                                anchorClass: "page-link",
                                onPageClick: (e, page) => {
                                    let idsModel = $('#products-tab').attr('data-ids').split(",")
                                    modelLoadPageOrderby(page, idsModel)
                                }
                            });
                            if (startFilterNew == 1) {
                                $('#page-selection-orderby').twbsPagination('destroy')
                                $('#page-selection-orderby').twbsPagination({
                                    totalPages: tongSotrang,
                                    startPage: 1,
                                    visiblePages: 5,
                                    first: 'First',
                                    prev: '<',
                                    next: '>',
                                    last: 'Last',
                                    href: false,
                                    pageClass: "page-item",
                                    anchorClass: "page-link",
                                    onPageClick: (e, page) => {
                                        let idsModel = $('#products-tab').attr('data-ids').split(",")
                                        modelLoadPageOrderby(page, idsModel)
                                        //$('html, body').animate({
                                        //    scrollTop: $("#products-tab").offset().top
                                        //}, 200)
                                    }
                                })
                                return
                            }
                        }
                    })
                ReloadBlockModels = 0
            }
        }

                    let cancelText = arrThamSoSplit[i].split("_")[0]
                    var params = cancelText.replace('params=', '').split(';')

                        var paramArr = param.split(':')
                        var paramName = paramArr[0]
                        var paramValue = paramArr[1]

                            if (paramName == (i)) {
                                inputs.push({
                                    Col: i,
                                    IDs: paramValue.split(',')
                                })

                    });

            if (checkStock) {
                LocCoSan += `1`
            }

            } else if (checkSale) {
                spNewSaleGood = `khuyen-mai`
            } else if (checkGood) {
                spNewSaleGood = `gia-tot`
            }
            if (TangGiam == '1') {
                SapXepTheoOrderBy += 'DESC'
            }

            if (vbIDHangSX) {
                vbHangSX.push(vbIDHangSX)

                } else if (filterParams == 100002) {

                } else if (filterParams == 100004) {

        const addParamsUrl = (param) => {       
            var fullUrl = $(location).attr('href')  
            var urlGoc = fullUrl.split('?')[0].split('page')[0]
            var queryString = fullUrl.split('?')[1]
            const data = {}
            var url = ''
            if (queryString) {   
                let arrPush = []
                const thamSo = param.split('=')
                const queries = queryString.split("&")
                let spec = []
                let specText = []
                let arrHang = []
                let list = []
                let stock = []
                let LuaChonSapXep = []
                let SapXepTangGiam = []
                let CheDoHienThi = []
                let inputs = []
                let ThamSoDuocDung = 0                
                queries.map(o => {
                    let splitParams = o.split('_')[0]
                    let splitTextParams = o.split('_')[1]
                    const path = splitParams.split("=")
                    if (path.length == 2) {
                        if (path[0] == 'm') {
                            arrHang.push(path[1].split(','))      
                            if (thamSo[0] == 'm') {                
                                arrHang.push(thamSo[1])
                                ThamSoDuocDung = 1
                            }
                        } else if (path[0] == `params`) {
                            let arrSpec = path[1].split(';')
                            for (i = 0; i < arrSpec.length; i++) {
                                spec.push({
                                    Col: arrSpec[i].split(':')[0],
                                    IDs: arrSpec[i].split(':')[1].split(',')
                                })
                            }
                            // text trong Params
                            if (splitTextParams) {
                                let arrTextParams = splitTextParams.split(';')
                                for (i = 0; i < arrTextParams.length; i++) {
                                    let T_spec = arrTextParams[i].split(":")[0]
                                    let T_data = arrTextParams[i].split(":")[1]
                                    specText.push({
                                        Name: T_spec,
                                        Values: T_data
                                    })
                                }
                            }
                            if (/^s\d+/.test(thamSo[0])) {       // chưa dùng: thêm bộ lọc với thông số chọn trong dropdown
                                spec.push({
                                    Col: thamSo[0].replace('s', ''),
                                    IDs: thamSo[1].split(',')
                                })
                                ThamSoDuocDung = 1
                            }
                        } else if (path[0] == 'ls') {
                            list.push(path[1])
                            if (thamSo[0] == 'ls') {              
                                list.push(thamSo[1])
                                ThamSoDuocDung = 1
                            }
                        } else if (path[0] == 'inStock') {
                            stock.push(path[1])
                            if (thamSo[0] == 'inStock') {             
                                stock.push(thamSo[1])
                                ThamSoDuocDung = 1
                            }
                        } else if (path[0] == 'productOrderBy') {
                            if (thamSo[0] == 'productOrderBy') {             
                                LuaChonSapXep.push(thamSo[1])
                                ThamSoDuocDung = 1
                            } else {
                                LuaChonSapXep.push(path[1])
                            }
                        } else if (path[0] == 'productUpDown') {
                            if (thamSo[0] == 'productUpDown') {             
                                SapXepTangGiam.push(thamSo[1])
                                ThamSoDuocDung = 1
                            } else {
                                SapXepTangGiam.push(path[1])
                            }
                        } else if (path[0] == 'activeView') {
                            if (thamSo[0] == 'activeView') {
                                CheDoHienThi.push(thamSo[1])
                                ThamSoDuocDung = 1
                            } else {
                                CheDoHienThi.push(path[1])
                            }
                        } else {
                            data[path[0]] = path[1]
                        }
                    }
                })
                data['HangSX'] = arrHang
                data['Spec'] = spec
                data['SpecText'] = specText
                data['ls'] = list
                data['inStock'] = stock
                data['productOrderBy'] = LuaChonSapXep
                data['productUpDown'] = SapXepTangGiam
                data['activeView'] = CheDoHienThi

                if (data.HangSX && data.HangSX.length) {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'm',
                        Value: data.HangSX
                    })
                }
                let TextParamsSpec = ``
                if (data.SpecText && data.SpecText.length) {
                    let text = []
                    data.SpecText.map((i) => {
                        if (i.Values.length) {
                            text.push(i.Name + `:` + i.Values)
                        }
                    })
                    TextParamsSpec += text.join(`;`)
                }
                if (data.Spec && data.Spec.length) {
                    let ts = []
                    data.Spec.map(o => {
                        if (o.IDs.length) {
                            ts.push(o.Col + `:` + o.IDs.join(","))
                        }
                    })
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: `params`,
                        Value: ts.join(`;`) + (TextParamsSpec ? `_` + TextParamsSpec : ``)
                    })
                }
                if (data.ls && data.ls.length) {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'ls',
                        Value: data.ls
                    })
                }
                if (data.inStock && data.inStock.length) {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'inStock',
                        Value: data.inStock
                    })
                }
                if (data.productOrderBy && data.productOrderBy.length) {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'productOrderBy',
                        Value: data.productOrderBy
                    })
                }
                if (data.productUpDown && data.productUpDown.length) {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'productUpDown',
                        Value: data.productUpDown
                    })
                }
                if (data.activeView && data.activeView.length) {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'activeView',
                        Value: data.activeView
                    })
                }
                if (ThamSoDuocDung == 0 && thamSo[0] == 'ls') {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'ls',
                        Value: thamSo[1]
                    })
                }
                if (ThamSoDuocDung == 0 && thamSo[0] == 'inStock') {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'inStock',
                        Value: thamSo[1]
                    })
                }
                if (ThamSoDuocDung == 0 && thamSo[0] == 'productOrderBy') {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'productOrderBy',
                        Value: thamSo[1]
                    })
                }
                if (ThamSoDuocDung == 0 && thamSo[0] == 'productUpDown') {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'productUpDown',
                        Value: thamSo[1]
                    })
                }
                if (ThamSoDuocDung == 0 && thamSo[0] == 'activeView') {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'activeView',
                        Value: thamSo[1]
                    })
                }
                let strInput  = ''
                inputs.map(k => {
                    if (strInput != '') {   
                        strInput += '&'
                    }
                    strInput += k.Name + '=' + k.Value
                })
                url = strInput != '' ? urlGoc + '?' + strInput : urlGoc
            } else {
                url = urlGoc + '?' + param
            }
            return url
        }
        const removeParamsUrl = (param) => {
            var url = ''
            var fullUrl = $(location).attr('href')
            var urlGoc = fullUrl.split('?')[0]
            var queryString = fullUrl.split('?')[1]
            const data = {}
            var url = ''
            if (queryString) {
                const thamSo = param.split('=')
                const queries = queryString.split("&")
                let arrHang = []
                let spec = []
                let specText = []
                let list = []
                let stock = []
                let LuaChonSapXep = []
                let SapXepTangGiam = []
                let CheDoHienThi = []
                let inputs = []
                let ThamSoDuocDung = 0              
                queries.map(o => {
                    let splitParams = o.split('_')[0]
                    let splitTextParams = o.split('_')[1]
                    const path = splitParams.split("=")
                    if (path.length == 2) {
                        if (path[0] == 'm') {
                            path[1].split(",").map(k => {      
                                if (k == thamSo[1]) {
                                } else {
                                    arrHang.push(k)
                                }
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == `params`) {
                            let arrTS = path[1].split(";")
                            for (i = 0; i < arrTS.length; i++) {
                                let S_spec = arrTS[i].split(":")[0]
                                let S_data = arrTS[i].split(":")[1]
                                let exitMap = 0
                                S_data.split(`,`).map(k => {
                                    if (S_spec != thamSo[0] && exitMap == 0) {
                                        spec.push({
                                            Col: S_spec,
                                            IDs: S_data.split(',')
                                        })
                                        exitMap = 1
                                    } else if (k == thamSo[1] && exitMap == 0) {
                                        //
                                    } else if (exitMap == 0) {
                                        spec.push({
                                            Col: thamSo[0].replace('s', ''),
                                            IDs: thamSo[1].split(',')
                                        })
                                    }
                                })
                            }
                            // text trong Params
                            if (splitTextParams) {
                                let arrTextParams = splitTextParams.split(';')
                                for (i = 0; i < arrTextParams.length; i++) {
                                    let T_spec = arrTextParams[i].split(":")[0]
                                    let T_data = arrTextParams[i].split(":")[1]
                                    specText.push({
                                        Name: T_spec,
                                        Values: T_data
                                    })
                                }
                            }
                        } else if (path[0] == 'ls') {
                            path[1].split(",").map(k => {       
                                if (path[0] != thamSo[0]) {
                                    list.push(path[1])
                                } else if (k == thamSo[1]) {
                                    //
                                } else {
                                    list.push(thamSo[1])
                                }
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == 'inStock') {
                            path[1].split(",").map(k => {     
                                if (path[0] != thamSo[0]) {
                                    stock.push(path[1])
                                } else if (k == thamSo[1]) {
                                    //
                                } else {
                                    stock.push(thamSo[1])
                                }
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == 'productOrderBy') {
                            path[1].split(",").map(k => {        
                                if (path[0] != thamSo[0]) {
                                    LuaChonSapXep.push(path[1])
                                } else if (k == thamSo[1] || thamSo[1] == '100001') {
                                    //
                                } else {
                                    LuaChonSapXep.push(thamSo[1])
                                }
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == 'productUpDown') {
                            path[1].split(",").map(k => {        
                                if (path[0] != thamSo[0]) {
                                    SapXepTangGiam.push(path[1])
                                } else if (k == thamSo[1] || thamSo[1] == '1') {
                                    //
                                } else {
                                    SapXepTangGiam.push(thamSo[1])
                                }
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == 'activeView') {
                            path[1].split(",").map(k => {
                                if (path[0] != thamSo[0]) {
                                    CheDoHienThi.push(path[1])
                                } else if (k == thamSo[1] || thamSo[1] == '1') {
                                    //
                                } else {
                                    CheDoHienThi.push(thamSo[1])
                                }
                            })
                        } else {
                            data[path[0]] = path[1]
                        }
                    }
                })
                data['HangSX'] = arrHang
                data['Spec'] = spec
                data['SpecText'] = specText
                data['ls'] = list
                data['inStock'] = stock
                data['productOrderBy'] = LuaChonSapXep
                data['productUpDown'] = SapXepTangGiam
                data['activeView'] = CheDoHienThi
                if (data.HangSX && data.HangSX.length) {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'm',
                        Value: data.HangSX
                    })
                }
                let TextParamsSpec = ``
                if (data.SpecText && data.SpecText.length) {
                    let text = []
                    data.SpecText.map((i) => {
                        if (i.Values.length) {
                            text.push(i.Name + `:` + i.Values)
                        }
                    })
                    TextParamsSpec += text.join(`;`)
                }
                if (data.Spec && data.Spec.length) {
                    let ts = []
                    data.Spec.map(o => {
                        if (o.IDs.length) {
                            ts.push(o.Col + `:` + o.IDs.join(","))
                        }
                    })
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: `params`,
                        Value: ts.join(`;`) + (TextParamsSpec ? `_` + TextParamsSpec : ``)
                    })
                }
                if (data.ls && data.ls.length) {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'ls',
                        Value: data.ls
                    })
                }
                if (data.inStock && data.inStock.length) {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'inStock',
                        Value: data.inStock
                    })
                }
                if (data.productOrderBy && data.productOrderBy.length) {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'productOrderBy',
                        Value: data.productOrderBy
                    })
                }
                if (data.productUpDown && data.productUpDown.length) {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'productUpDown',
                        Value: data.productUpDown
                    })
                }
                if (data.activeView && data.activeView.length) {
                    inputs.push({
                        Name: 'activeView',
                        Value: data.activeView
                    })
                }
                let strInput = ''
                inputs.map(k => {
                    if (strInput != '') {         
                        strInput += '&'
                    }
                    strInput += k.Name + '=' + k.Value
                })
                url = strInput != '' ? urlGoc + '?' + strInput : urlGoc
            }
            return url
        }
        const loadSeries = (id, ls, total, filterList) => {
            if (vbTenHangSX) {
                axios.post(`/api/UtilsApi/cate-search-loading`, { lang: vbLang, id: id, series: ls, filter: { List: filterList, key: vbKey, Point: vbPoint, HangSXSearchID: { ID: vbIDHangSX, Ten: vbTenHangSX, TenSlugHangSX: vbTenSlugHangSX }, HangSXSearch: vbTenHangSX } })
                    .then(function (response) {
                        if (response.data.data) {
                            renderSeriesOfCate(id, response.data.data, total)
                        }
                    })
            } else {
                axios.post(`/api/UtilsApi/cate-search-loading`, { lang: vbLang, id: id, series: ls, filter: { List: filterList, key: vbKey, Point: vbPoint } })
                    .then(function (response) {
                        if (response.data.data) {
                            renderSeriesOfCate(id, response.data.data, total)
                        }
                    })
            }
        }
        const renderSeriesOfCate = (id, data, total) => {
            $(`.searching--cate-loading-title${id}`).text(data.Ten)
            $(`.searching--cate-link-loading-title${id}`).attr("href", data.Link)
            $(`.searching--cate-loading-number${id}`).removeClass('d-none')
            $(`.searching--cate-loading[data-id="${id}"] .seri-loadmore`).remove()
            data.Series.map(sp => {
                let ship = ``
                if (sp.TonBAC) {
                    ship += `<i class="bi bi-check2-square mx-2 fs-3"></i><span class="product__card--ship-content-label">${vbLangImmediately}</span>`
                } else if (sp.TonNCC > 0 && sp.DaCoNCC && (sp.CoSanTu || sp.CoSanDen)) {
                    ship += `<i class="bi bi-check2-square mx-2 fs-3"></i><span class="product__card--ship-content-label">${sp.CoSanTu}${sp.CoSanDen ? `~ ${sp.CoSanDen}` : ``}&nbsp;${vbLangDays}</span>`
                } else if ((sp.TonNCC == 0 || !sp.TonNCC) && (sp.DatHangTu || sp.DatHangDen)) {
                    ship += `<i class="bi bi-envelope mx-2 fs-3"></i><span class="product__card--ship-content-label">${sp.DatHangTu}${sp.DatHangDen ? `~ ${sp.DatHangDen}` : ``}&nbsp;${vbLangDays}</span>`
                } else {
                    ship += `<i class="bi bi-envelope mx-2 fs-3"></i><span class="product__card--ship-content-label">${vbLangContactMe}</span>`
                }
                $(`.searching--cate-loading[data-id="${id}"]`).append(`<div class="col position-relative m-0 p-0">
                        <a class="card product__card" href="${sp.Link}">
                            <div class="position-absolute product__card--img">
                                <div class="form-image">
                                    ${sp.PictureBAA ? `<img class="card-img-top height_auto" loading="lazy" width="300" height="300" src="${vbPathSeries + id + `/160/`}${sp.PictureBAA}" alt="${sp.Name}">` : `<img class="card-img-top form-image" loading="lazy" width="300" height="300" src="https://baoanjsc.com.vn/Images/nosanphamX.jpg" alt="...">`}
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="card-body px-2 py-0">
                                <div class="product__card--body3">
                                    <p class="product__card--title">
                                        <span class="product__card--title-span d-webkit-box-3">${sp.Name}${sp.TenHangSanXuat ? ` ${sp.TenHangSanXuat}` : ``}${sp.Series ? ` ${sp.Series}` : ``}</span>
                                    </p>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </a>
                        <div class=" row pb-2 px-2 d-flex justify-content-between position-absolute divGiaoHang_Favourite_Cart">
                            <div class=" product__card--ship-icon align-items-center d-flex" title="${vbDeliveryTime}">
                                
                                <span class="product__card--ship-content align-items-center d-flex">
                                    ${ship}
                                </span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>`)
                })
                if ($(`.searching--cate-loading[data-id="${id}"]`).children().length < total) {
                    $(`.searching--cate-loading[data-id="${id}"]`).append(`<div class="col seri-loadmore">
                        <div class="card product__card h-100">
                            <div class="position-absolute product__card--img h-100 w-100 d-flex justify-content-center align-items-center">
                                <i class="bi bi-boxes text-success loadmore--icon"></i>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>`)
                }
            }
        const getAllModelCompare = (status) => {
            axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/get-data-model-compare', { Status: status, Lang: vbLang })
                .then(function (response) {
                    let vbCompare =`So sánh`
                    let vbLinkCompare = `/vn/compare/`
                    if (response.data.length == 0) {
                        if (!$('.show_compare-model').hasClass('d-none')) {
                            $('.show_compare-model').addClass('d-none')
                        }
                        return
                    }
                    if ($('.show_compare-model').hasClass('d-none')) {
                        $('.show_compare-model').removeClass('d-none')
                    }
                    $('.row-items_model').empty()
                    let html_compare_footer = ``
                    let countModel = 0
                    let alowCountModel = 3
                    response.data.map(o => {
                        if (countModel < alowCountModel) {
                            html_compare_footer += `<div class="item_model">
                                                <div class="">
                                                    ${o.HinhAnh != '' ? `<img class="img_model" loading="lazy" src="${o.LinkHinhAnh + `160/` + o.HinhAnh}" Title="${o.Model}" alt="${o.Model}" />` : `<img class="img_model" loading="lazy" src="${vbPathImageBAA}nosanphamX.jpg" alt="Bao An Automation">` }
                                                </div>
                                                <button class="model_delete-compare btn-close" Title="Delete" data-id="${o.ID}" type="button" >
                                                </button>
                                            </div>`
                        }
                        countModel += 1
                    })
                    html_compare_footer += countModel > alowCountModel ? `<a class="model_compare-more" href="${vbLinkCompare}" aria-label="model compare">
                                                            <span class="model_compare-more-plus">+</span>
                                                            <span class="model_compare-more-count">${countModel - alowCountModel}</span>
                                                        </a>` : ``
                    html_compare_footer += `<a class="btn btn_compare_modal-footer model_compare-button p-0" href="${vbLinkCompare}" aria-label="${vbCompare}">
                                                        <span>${vbCompare}</span>
                                                    </a>`
                    $('.row-items_model').append(html_compare_footer)
                })
        }

        $('.baaFilter').on('input propertychange', '.filterTop--search', function () {
            const id = $(this).parents('.widget_Items').data('id')
            if ($(this).val()) {
                const search = removeAccents($(this).val().toLowerCase())
                $(`.widget_Items[data-id="${id}"] .itemLabel`).each(function () {
                    if (removeAccents($(this).text().toLowerCase()).indexOf(search) == -1) {
                        if (!$(this).parents('.widget_Item').hasClass('d-none')) {
                            $(this).parents('.widget_Item').addClass('d-none')
                        }
                    } else {
                        $(this).parents('.widget_Item').removeClass('d-none')
                    }
                })
            } else {
                $(`.widget_Items[data-id="${id}"] .widget_Item`).removeClass('d-none')
            }
        })

                $(`.filter-box-item-label`).each(function () {
                    if (removeAccents($(this).text().toLowerCase()).indexOf(search) == -1) {
                        if (!$(this).parents('.filter-box-item').hasClass('d-none')) {
                            $(this).parents('.filter-box-item').addClass('d-none')

        $('.btn-filter--add-apply').on('click', function () {
            let IdFiltered = []
            $(`.contentFilter .widget_Items`).each(function () {
                let id = $(this).data('id')
                IdFiltered.push(id)
            })
            let strFiltered = ',' + IdFiltered.join(',') + ','
            let IDsDelete = []
            $(`.filter-box-item-input`).each(function () {
                let id = $(this).val()
                if ($(this).is(":checked")) {
                    if (strFiltered.includes(',' + id + ',') || strFiltered.includes(',s' + id + ',')) {

                    } else {
                        IdFiltered.push('s' + id)
                    }
                } else {
                    if (strFiltered.includes(',' + id + ',')) {
                        _.remove(IdFiltered, function (e) {
                            return e === (id);
                        })
                        IDsDelete.push(id)
                    } else if (strFiltered.includes(',s' + id + ',')) {
                        _.remove(IdFiltered, function (e) {
                            return e === ('s' + id);
                        })
                        IDsDelete.push(id)
                    } else {
                    }
                }
            })
            let reloadPage = false
            if (IDsDelete.length > 0) {
                let arrThamSo = []
                let url = window.location.pathname
                let ThamSo = window.location.search
                if (ThamSo != '') {
                    ThamSo = ThamSo.replace('?', '')
                    arrThamSo = ThamSo.split("&")
                }
                let a = []
                for (i = 0; i < arrThamSo.length; i++) {
                    const path = arrThamSo[i].split("=")
                    if ($.inArray(`${path[0].replace(`s`, ``)}`, IDsDelete) == -1) {
                        a.push(`${arrThamSo[i]}`)
                    }
                }
                let b = a.join('&')
                if (ThamSo != b) {
                    reloadPage = true
                    window.location.href = url + '?' + b
                }
            }
            if (!reloadPage) {
                let SapXepIds = IdFiltered.join(',')
                let strHangCateSeri = `m,Cate,Seri,`
                addAllFilter += strHangCateSeri + SapXepIds.replaceAll(strHangCateSeri, '').replaceAll('s', '')
                getAddFilter()
            }
            $('#filter__box').modal('hide')
        })

                let id = $(this).data('id')

                checkNewModel = $('#checkerLableNew:checked').val() ? 1 : 0
                checkSaleModel = $('#checkerLableSale:checked').val() ? 1 : 0
                checkGoodModel = $('#checkerLableGood:checked').val() ? 1 : 0

                orderby = $("#OrderByAscDescs option:selected").val()
                checkToShowModelFilter(checkStockModel, checkNewModel, checkSaleModel, checkGoodModel, filterModelParams, orderby, `1`)
                window.history.replaceState(null, null, removeParamsUrl('ls=moi'));
                getFilter()
                enableUI()
            }
            startFilterNew = 1
        })

        $('.ChooseFilter-remove-all').on('click', function () {
            disableUI()
            var fullUrl = $(location).attr('href')
            var urlGoc = fullUrl.split('?')[0].split('page')[0]
            var queryString = fullUrl.split('?')[1]
            var url = ''
            if (queryString) {
                let inputs = []
                const queries = queryString.split("&")
                queries.map(o => {
                    let splitParams = o.split('_')[0]
                    const path = splitParams.split("=")
                    if (path.length == 2) {
                        if (path[0] == 'm') {
                            inputs.push({
                                Name: 'm',
                                Value: path[1]
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == `params`) { //bỏ qua tham số Params
                        } else if (path[0] == 'ls') {
                            inputs.push({
                                Name: 'ls',
                                Value: path[1]
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == 'inStock') {
                            inputs.push({
                                Name: 'inStock',
                                Value: path[1]
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == 'productOrderBy') {
                            inputs.push({
                                Name: 'productOrderBy',
                                Value: path[1]
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == 'productUpDown') {
                            inputs.push({
                                Name: 'productUpDown',
                                Value: path[1]
                            })
                        } else {
                            //
                        }
                    }
                })
                let strInput = ''
                inputs.map(k => {
                    if (strInput != '') {
                        strInput += '&'
                    }
                    strInput += k.Name + '=' + k.Value
                })
                url = strInput != '' ? urlGoc + '?' + strInput : urlGoc
            } else {
                url = urlGoc
            }
            window.location.href = url;
        })
        $('.btnCloseParam').on('click', function () {
            let s = $(this).data('s')
            let id = $(this).data('id')
            let TextTitle = $(this).data('texttitle')
            let TextValue = $(this).data('textvalue')
            var fullUrl = $(location).attr('href')
            var urlGoc = fullUrl.split('?')[0].split('page')[0]
            var queryString = fullUrl.split('?')[1]
            var url = ''
            if (queryString) {
                let inputs = []
                let specText = []
                let getTextParams = []
                let countParams = 0
                const queries = queryString.split("&")
                let arrTextParams = vbTextParamsUrl
                arrTextParams = arrTextParams ? arrTextParams.split(";") : ``
                if (arrTextParams.length) {
                    arrTextParams.map((e) => {
                        getTextParams.push({
                            Name: e.split(':')[0],
                            values: e.split(':')[1].split(',')
                        })
                    })
                }
                queries.map(o => {
                    let splitParams = o.split('_')[0]
                    let splitTextParams = o.split('_')[1]
                    const path = splitParams.split("=")
                    if (path.length == 2) {
                        if (path[0] == 'm') {
                            inputs.push({
                                Name: 'm',
                                Value: path[1]
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == `params`) { 
                            let spec = []
                            let TextParamsSpec = ``
                            let arrTS = path[1].split(";")
                            for (i = 0; i < arrTS.length; i++) {
                                let IDs=[]
                                let S_spec = arrTS[i].split(":")[0]
                                let S_data = arrTS[i].split(":")[1]
                                countParams += S_data.split(',').length
                                if (S_spec == s) {
                                    S_data.split(`,`).map(k => {
                                        if (k != id) {
                                            IDs.push(k)
                                        } else {
                                            //
                                        }
                                    })
                                    if (IDs.length) {
                                        spec.push({
                                            Col: S_spec,
                                            IDs: IDs.join(",")
                                        })
                                    }
                                } else {
                                    spec.push({
                                        Col: S_spec,
                                        IDs: S_data
                                    })
                                }
                            }
                            let EachTextParam = $.extend(true, [], getTextParams)
                            if (splitTextParams) {
                                let arrTextParams = splitTextParams.split(';')
                                for (i = 0; i < arrTextParams.length; i++) {
                                    let T_spec = arrTextParams[i].split(":")[0]
                                    let T_data = arrTextParams[i].split(":")[1]
                                    if (T_spec == TextTitle) {
                                        let arr_T_data = T_data.split(',')
                                        let arrValue = []
                                        arr_T_data.map(t => {
                                            if (t != TextValue) {
                                                arrValue.push(t)
                                            }
                                        })
                                        if (arrValue.length) {
                                            specText.push({
                                                Name: T_spec,
                                                Values: arrValue.join(',')
                                            })
                                        }
                                    } else {
                                        specText.push({
                                            Name: T_spec,
                                            Values: T_data
                                        })
                                    }
                                }
                            } else {
                                let arrRemoveText = []
                                if (countParams <= 3) {
                                    EachTextParam.map((k) => {
                                        if (TextTitle == k.Name) {
                                            var index = k.values.indexOf(TextValue)
                                            if (index > -1) {
                                                k.values.splice(index, 1)
                                                if (k.values.length > 0) {
                                                    arrRemoveText.push(k)
                                                }
                                            } else {
                                                arrRemoveText.push(k)
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            arrRemoveText.push(k)
                                        }
                                    }
                                    )
                                }

                                EachTextParam = []
                                EachTextParam = arrRemoveText
                                if (EachTextParam.length) {
                                    // nếu có 1 tham số thì thêm tham số này vào url
                                    EachTextParam.map((e) => {
                                        TextParamsSpec += TextParamsSpec != `` ? `;` : ``
                                        TextParamsSpec += e.Name + ':' + e.values.join(',')
                                    })
                                }
                            }
                            if (specText.length) {
                                let ts = []
                                specText.map(s => {
                                    if (s.Values.length) {
                                        ts.push(s.Name + `:` + s.Values)
                                    }
                                })
                                TextParamsSpec += ts.join(';')
                            }
                            if (spec.length) {
                                let ts = []
                                spec.map(o => {
                                    if (o.IDs.length) {
                                        ts.push(o.Col + `:` + o.IDs)
                                    }
                                })
                                inputs.push({
                                    Name: `params`,
                                    Value: ts.join(`;`) + (TextParamsSpec ? `_` + TextParamsSpec : ``)
                                })
                            }
                        } else if (path[0] == 'ls') {
                            inputs.push({
                                Name: 'ls',
                                Value: path[1]
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == 'inStock') {
                            inputs.push({
                                Name: 'inStock',
                                Value: path[1]
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == 'productOrderBy') {
                            inputs.push({
                                Name: 'productOrderBy',
                                Value: path[1]
                            })
                        } else if (path[0] == 'productUpDown') {
                            inputs.push({
                                Name: 'productUpDown',
                                Value: path[1]
                            })
                        } else {
                            //
                        }
                    }
                })
                let strInput = ''
                inputs.map(k => {
                    if (strInput != '') {
                        strInput += '&'
                    }
                    strInput += k.Name + '=' + k.Value
                })
                url = strInput != '' ? urlGoc + '?' + strInput : urlGoc
            } else {
                url = urlGoc
            }
            window.location.href = url;
        })
        $('.models-loading').on('click', '.btnAddToCompare-modul-ctsp', function () {
            let $this = $(this)
            var id = $this.attr('data-id')
            var status = $this.attr('data-status')
            axios.post('/api/UtilsApi/check-add-remove-to-compare', { ID: id, Status: status })
                .then(function (response) {
                    if (response.data.data == 0) {
                        $this.attr('data-status', 1)
                        $this.attr('title', vbRemoveCompare)
                        $(`.icon-ctsp_${id}`).empty()
                        $(`.icon-ctsp_${id}`).append('<svg class="i-icon o-icon--small" data-modifier=""><use xlink:href="#compare-icon-active-svg"></use></svg>')
                        getAllModelCompare(1)
                    } else if (response.data.data == 1) {
                        $this.attr('data-status', 0)
                        $this.attr('title', vbAddToCompare)
                        $(`.icon-ctsp_${id}`).empty()
                        $(`.icon-ctsp_${id}`).append('<svg class="i-icon o-icon--small" data-modifier=""><use xlink:href="#compare-icon-svg"></use></svg>')
                        getAllModelCompare(1)
                    }
                })
            var data = {
                message: 'message_channel',
                id: id,
                status: status
            }
            channel.postMessage(JSON.stringify(data))
        })

        $(document).ready(function (id) {
            //$('.loadingGray').removeClass('d-none')
            var ParamCoSan = 0
            var ParamNew = 0
            var ParamSale = 0
            var ParamGood = 0
            var ParamProductOrderBy = 0
            var ParamProductUpDown = 0
            if (vbInStock == `1`) {
                $('#checkerLableAvailable').prop('checked', true);
                ParamCoSan = 1
            }
            if (vbList == `moi`) {
                $('#checkerLableNew').prop('checked', true);
                $('#checkerLableSale').attr('disabled', true)
                $('#checkerLableGood').attr('disabled', true)
                ParamNew = 1
            } else if (vbList == `khuyen-mai`) {
                $('#checkerLableSale').prop('checked', true);
                $('#checkerLableNew').attr('disabled', true)
                $('#checkerLableGood').attr('disabled', true)
                ParamSale = 1

                $('#checkerLableGood').prop('checked', true);
                $('#checkerLableNew').attr('disabled', true)
                $('#checkerLableSale').attr('disabled', true)
                ParamGood = 1
            }
            if (vbProductOrderBy) {
                $(`#OrderByModelParams option[value=${vbProductOrderBy}]`).attr('selected', 'selected')
                ParamProductOrderBy = vbProductOrderBy
            }
            if (vbProductUpDown) {
                $(`#OrderByAscDescs option[value=${vbProductUpDown}]`).attr('selected', 'selected')
                ParamProductUpDown = vbProductUpDown
            }
            if (window.innerWidth > 1024 && vbSeri != null) {
                if ($('.btn_list-table').hasClass('d-none')) {
                    $('.btn_list-table').removeClass('d-none')
                }
            }
            if (vbActiveView) {
                $('#checkerLableAvailable').attr('disabled', true)
                $('#checkerLableNew').attr('disabled', true)
                $('#checkerLableSale').attr('disabled', true)
                $('#checkerLableGood').attr('disabled', true)

                $('.btn-list-table_icon[data-view=block]').attr(`data-active`, `false`)
                customDatatables()

                    var scrollLeft = $(this).scrollLeft();

                    $('.dataTables_paginate').parents('.row').css('position', 'relative');
                    $('.dataTables_length').parents('.row').css('left', scrollLeft + 'px');
                    $('.dataTables_length').parents('.row').css('position', 'relative');
                });
            } else {
                if ($('.filter-params-orderby').hasClass('d-none')) {
                    $('.filter-params-orderby').removeClass('d-none')
                }
            }
            checkToShowModelFilter(ParamCoSan, ParamNew, ParamSale, ParamGood, ParamProductOrderBy, ParamProductUpDown,`0`)
            if (models.length && `` != ``) {
                var urlRun = vbUrlAbsolute.split("page")[0] + `page/{{number}}/` + vbUrlQuery
                urlRun = decodeURIComponent(urlRun)     //.replace('%2c', ',').replace('%3a', ':').replace('%3b', ';')

                const TrangBatDau = vbIdPage < tongSotrang ? vbIdPage : tongSotrang

                    totalPages: tongSotrang,

                    visiblePages: 5,

                    prev: '<',
                    next : '>',
                    last: 'Last',

                        if (`` != ``) {
                            modelLoadPage(page)

                            //    scrollTop: $(".container-fluid").offset().top
                            //}, 200)
                        }
                    }
                });

            if (vbKey && vbKey != ``) {
                $('.loadingGray').addClass('d-none')
                modelLoadPage(1)
            }
            $('.searching--cate-loading').each(function () {
                const id = $(this).data('id')
                const filterList= $(this).data('list')
                const series = $(this).data('series').toString()
                const arSr = series.split(',')
                let ls = []
                if (arSr.length < 8) {
                    ls = _.chunk(arSr, 7)
                } else {
                    ls = _.chunk(arSr, 6)
                }
                if (ls.length) {
                    loadSeries(id, ls[0], arSr.length,filterList)
                }
            })
            //if (vbDsBaiViet.length) {
            //    $('#page-selection-news').twbsPagination({
            //        initiateStartPageClick: false,
            //        totalPages: Math.ceil(models.length / 20),
            //        startPage: modelsPage,
            //        visiblePages: 5,
